## Diagram 3

```mermaid
graph LR
    Strategies[Descheduler Strategies]
    
    Strategies --> RemoveDup[RemoveDuplicates]
    RemoveDup --> DupEnabled[Enabled]
    
    Strategies --> RemoveRestarts[RemovePodsHavingTooManyRestarts]
    RemoveRestarts --> RestartThreshold[Threshold: 100 restarts]
    
    Strategies --> RemoveTaints[RemovePodsViolatingNodeTaints]
    RemoveTaints --> TaintsEnabled[Enabled]
    
    Strategies --> RemoveAffinity[RemovePodsViolatingNodeAffinity]
    RemoveAffinity --> AffinityType[requiredDuringScheduling]
    
    Strategies --> RemoveAntiAffinity[RemovePodsViolatingInterPodAntiAffinity]
    RemoveAntiAffinity --> AntiAffinityEnabled[Enabled]
    
    Strategies --> RemoveTopology[RemovePodsViolatingTopologySpreadConstraint]
    RemoveTopology --> TopologyEnabled[Enabled]
    
    Strategies --> LowUtil[LowNodeUtilization]
    LowUtil --> Thresholds[CPU:20% Memory:20% Pods:20%]
    LowUtil --> Targets[CPU:50% Memory:50% Pods:50%]
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start([Descheduler Start])
    Start --> CheckKind{Deployment Kind?}
    
    CheckKind -->|CronJob| CronSchedule[Wait for Cron: */2 * * * *]
    CheckKind -->|Deployment| DeployLoop[Run every 5m]
    
    CronSchedule --> Execute[Execute Descheduling]
    DeployLoop --> Execute
    
    Execute --> CheckLeader{Leader Election?}
    CheckLeader -->|Yes| AmILeader{Am I Leader?}
    CheckLeader -->|No| RunStrategies[Run Strategies]
    
    AmILeader -->|Yes| RunStrategies
    AmILeader -->|No| Wait[Wait for next cycle]
    
    RunStrategies --> Strategy1[RemoveDuplicates]
    Strategy1 --> Strategy2[RemovePodsHavingTooManyRestarts]
    Strategy2 --> Strategy3[RemovePodsViolatingNodeTaints]
    Strategy3 --> Strategy4[RemovePodsViolatingNodeAffinity]
    Strategy4 --> Strategy5[RemovePodsViolatingInterPodAntiAffinity]
    Strategy5 --> Strategy6[RemovePodsViolatingTopologySpreadConstraint]
    Strategy6 --> Strategy7[LowNodeUtilization]
    
    Strategy7 --> EvictPods[Evict Pods]
    EvictPods --> End([End Cycle])
    End --> Wait
    Wait --> CheckKind
```

## Diagram 6

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class DeschedulerConfig {
        +String kind
        +Image image
        +Resources resources
        +SecurityContext securityContext
        +String schedule
        +String deschedulingInterval
        +int replicas
        +Policy deschedulerPolicy
    }
    
    class Image {
        +String repository
        +String tag
        +String pullPolicy
    }
    
    class Resources {
        +Map requests
        +Map limits
    }
    
    class SecurityContext {
        +boolean allowPrivilegeEscalation
        +Capabilities capabilities
        +boolean privileged
        +boolean readOnlyRootFilesystem
        +boolean runAsNonRoot
        +int runAsUser
    }
    
    class Policy {
        +String apiVersion
        +Strategies strategies
        +int maxNoOfPodsToEvictPerNode
        +int maxNoOfPodsToEvictPerNamespace
    }
    
    class Strategies {
        +RemoveDuplicates removeDuplicates
        +RemovePodsHavingTooManyRestarts removePodsHavingTooManyRestarts
        +RemovePodsViolatingNodeTaints removePodsViolatingNodeTaints
        +RemovePodsViolatingNodeAffinity removePodsViolatingNodeAffinity
        +RemovePodsViolatingInterPodAntiAffinity removePodsViolatingInterPodAntiAffinity
        +RemovePodsViolatingTopologySpreadConstraint removePodsViolatingTopologySpreadConstraint
        +LowNodeUtilization lowNodeUtilization
    }
    
    class RBAC {
        +boolean create
    }
    
    class ServiceAccount {
        +boolean create
        +String name
        +Map annotations
    }
    
    class Monitoring {
        +LivenessProbe livenessProbe
        +Service service
        +ServiceMonitor serviceMonitor
    }
    
    DeschedulerConfig --> Image
    DeschedulerConfig --> Resources
    DeschedulerConfig --> SecurityContext
    DeschedulerConfig --> Policy
    DeschedulerConfig --> RBAC
    DeschedulerConfig --> ServiceAccount
    DeschedulerConfig --> Monitoring
    Policy --> Strategies
```
